LAW DEPARTMENT
LIST OF NOTARIES APPOINTED AND IN PRACTICE AT THE BEGINNING OF THE YEAR 2019
(See rule 17) 
[G.O. Ms. No. 27, Law (Administration) Department, 31st January 2019.]
No. II(2)/LAW/117(b)/2019.
In exercise of the powers conferred by Section 6 of the Notaries Act, 1952 (Central Act LIII of 1952), the Governor 
of Tamil Nadu hereby publishes the following list of Notaries appointed by the Government of Tamil Nadu and in practice 
at the beginning of the year 2019 :—
